## File: bundle_project.js

```js
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const path = require('path');

// Thư mục dự án cần tổng hợp (thay bằng thư mục dự án của bạn nếu cần)
const projectDir = path.join(__dirname);
// Đường dẫn file đầu ra
const outputFile = path.join(__dirname, 'project_summary.txt');
// Các loại file cần tổng hợp (thêm hoặc bớt theo nhu cầu)
const fileExtensions = ['.js', '.jsx', '.ts', '.tsx', '.html', '.css', '.json'];

// Hàm kiểm tra xem file có nằm trong danh sách loại file cần tổng hợp không
function isValidFile(file) {
  return fileExtensions.includes(path.extname(file).toLowerCase());
}

// Hàm đệ quy để quét tất cả file trong thư mục
async function getAllFiles(dir, fileList = []) {
  const files = await fs.readdir(dir, { withFileTypes: true });
  
  for (const file of files) {
    const filePath = path.join(dir, file.name);
    if (file.isDirectory()) {
      // Bỏ qua các thư mục không cần thiết
      if (['node_modules', '.git', 'dist', 'build'].includes(file.name)) {
        continue;
      }
      await getAllFiles(filePath, fileList);
    } else if (isValidFile(file.name)) {
      fileList.push(filePath);
    }
  }
  return fileList;
}

// Hàm chính để tổng hợp nội dung
async function bundleProject() {
  try {
    console.log('Đang quét dự án...');
    const files = await getAllFiles(projectDir);
    
    let outputContent = '# Tổng hợp code dự án\n\n';
    for (const file of files) {
      try {
        const content = await fs.readFile(file, 'utf8');
        const relativePath = path.relative(__dirname, file);
        outputContent += `## File: ${relativePath}\n\n`;
        outputContent += '```' + path.extname(file).slice(1) + '\n';
        outputContent += content + '\n';
        outputContent += '```\n\n';
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`Lỗi khi đọc file ${file}:`, error);
      }
    }
    
    await fs.writeFile(outputFile, outputContent);
    console.log(`Đã tạo file tổng hợp tại: ${outputFile}`);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Lỗi khi tổng hợp dự án:', error);
  }
}

// Chạy hàm
bundleProject();
```

## File: src\app\bao-cao\page.tsx

```tsx
'use client';

import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Card, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Toaster, toast } from 'react-hot-toast';
import { format } from 'date-fns';
import { Pie, Bar } from 'react-chartjs-2';
import { Chart as ChartJS, ArcElement, Tooltip, Legend, CategoryScale, LinearScale, BarElement, Title } from 'chart.js';

ChartJS.register(ArcElement, Tooltip, Legend, CategoryScale, LinearScale, BarElement, Title);

interface BaoCao {
  mat: {
    doanhthu_thuoc: number;
    doanhthu_thuthuat: number;
    lai_thuoc: number;
    lai_thuthuat: number;
    no_thuoc: number;
    no_thuthuat: number;
  };
  tmh: {
    doanhthu_thuoc: number;
    doanhthu_thuthuat: number;
    lai_thuoc: number;
    lai_thuthuat: number;
    no_thuoc: number;
    no_thuthuat: number;
  };
  kinh: {
    doanhthu: number;
    lai: number;
    no: number;
  };
  chi_tiet: {
    mat: { thuoc: Array<{ id: number; ngay: string; doanhthu: number; lai: number; no: number }>; thuthuat: Array<{ id: number; ngay: string; doanhthu: number; lai: number; no: number }> };
    tmh: { thuoc: Array<{ id: number; ngay: string; doanhthu: number; lai: number; no: number }>; thuthuat: Array<{ id: number; ngay: string; doanhthu: number; lai: number; no: number }> };
    kinh: Array<{ id: number; ngay: string; doanhthu: number; lai: number; no: number }>;
  };
}

export default function BaoCaoPage() {
  const [baoCao, setBaoCao] = useState<BaoCao | null>(null);
  const [fromDate, setFromDate] = useState(format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd'));
  const [toDate, setToDate] = useState(format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd'));
  const [chuyenKhoa, setChuyenKhoa] = useState('');
  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1);
  const rowsPerPage = 10;

  const fetchBaoCao = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const res = await axios.get('/api/bao-cao', {
        params: { from: fromDate, to: toDate, chuyen_khoa: chuyenKhoa || undefined },
      });
      setBaoCao(res.data.data);
    } catch (error: unknown) {
      console.error('Lỗi khi gọi API bao-cao:', error);
      if (axios.isAxiosError(error)) {
        toast.error('Lỗi khi tải báo cáo: ' + (error.response?.data?.message || error.message));
      } else if (error instanceof Error) {
        toast.error('Lỗi khi tải báo cáo: ' + error.message);
      } else {
        toast.error('Lỗi không xác định khi tải báo cáo');
      }
    }
  }, [fromDate, toDate, chuyenKhoa]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchBaoCao();
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [fromDate, toDate, chuyenKhoa]);

  const chiTiet = baoCao
    ? [
        ...baoCao.chi_tiet.mat.thuoc.map((item) => ({ ...item, chuyen_khoa: 'Mắt', type: 'Thuốc' })),
        ...baoCao.chi_tiet.mat.thuthuat.map((item) => ({ ...item, chuyen_khoa: 'Mắt', type: 'Thủ thuật' })),
        ...baoCao.chi_tiet.tmh.thuoc.map((item) => ({ ...item, chuyen_khoa: 'TMH', type: 'Thuốc' })),
        ...baoCao.chi_tiet.tmh.thuthuat.map((item) => ({ ...item, chuyen_khoa: 'TMH', type: 'Thủ thuật' })),
        ...baoCao.chi_tiet.kinh.map((item) => ({ ...item, chuyen_khoa: 'Kính', type: 'Kính' })),
      ].filter((item) => !chuyenKhoa || item.chuyen_khoa === chuyenKhoa)
    : [];

  const totalPages = Math.ceil(chiTiet.length / rowsPerPage);
  const paginated = chiTiet.slice((currentPage - 1) * rowsPerPage, currentPage * rowsPerPage);

  // Biểu đồ tròn: Tỷ lệ doanh thu
  const doanhThuChartData = baoCao
    ? {
        labels: ['Mắt - Thuốc', 'Mắt - Thủ thuật', 'TMH - Thuốc', 'TMH - Thủ thuật', 'Kính'],
        datasets: [
          {
            label: 'Doanh thu (nghìn)',
            data: [
              baoCao.mat.doanhthu_thuoc / 1000,
              baoCao.mat.doanhthu_thuthuat / 1000,
              baoCao.tmh.doanhthu_thuoc / 1000,
              baoCao.tmh.doanhthu_thuthuat / 1000,
              baoCao.kinh.doanhthu / 1000,
            ],
            backgroundColor: [
              'rgba(75, 192, 192, 0.6)',
              'rgba(54, 162, 235, 0.6)',
              'rgba(255, 99, 132, 0.6)',
              'rgba(255, 206, 86, 0.6)',
              'rgba(153, 102, 255, 0.6)',
            ],
            borderColor: [
              'rgba(75, 192, 192, 1)',
              'rgba(54, 162, 235, 1)',
              'rgba(255, 99, 132, 1)',
              'rgba(255, 206, 86, 1)',
              'rgba(153, 102, 255, 1)',
            ],
            borderWidth: 1,
          },
        ],
      }
    : null;

  // Biểu đồ cột: Tổng lãi theo ngày
  const laiChartData = baoCao
    ? {
        labels: [...new Set([
          ...baoCao.chi_tiet.mat.thuoc.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
          ...baoCao.chi_tiet.mat.thuthuat.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
          ...baoCao.chi_tiet.tmh.thuoc.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
          ...baoCao.chi_tiet.tmh.thuthuat.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
          ...baoCao.chi_tiet.kinh.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
        ])].sort(),
        datasets: [
          {
            label: 'Tổng lãi (nghìn)',
            data: [...new Set([
              ...baoCao.chi_tiet.mat.thuoc.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
              ...baoCao.chi_tiet.mat.thuthuat.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
              ...baoCao.chi_tiet.tmh.thuoc.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
              ...baoCao.chi_tiet.tmh.thuthuat.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
              ...baoCao.chi_tiet.kinh.map(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')),
            ])].sort().map(date => {
              const totalLai = [
                ...baoCao.chi_tiet.mat.thuoc,
                ...baoCao.chi_tiet.mat.thuthuat,
                ...baoCao.chi_tiet.tmh.thuoc,
                ...baoCao.chi_tiet.tmh.thuthuat,
                ...baoCao.chi_tiet.kinh,
              ].filter(item => new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN') === date)
                .reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.lai, 0);
              return totalLai / 1000;
            }),
            backgroundColor: 'rgba(75, 192, 192, 0.6)',
            borderColor: 'rgba(75, 192, 192, 1)',
            borderWidth: 1,
          },
        ],
      }
    : null;

  // Tổng tỷ lệ lãi
  const tongTyLeLai = baoCao
    ? (((baoCao.mat.lai_thuoc + baoCao.mat.lai_thuthuat + baoCao.tmh.lai_thuoc + baoCao.tmh.lai_thuthuat + baoCao.kinh.lai) /
        (baoCao.mat.doanhthu_thuoc + baoCao.mat.doanhthu_thuthuat + baoCao.tmh.doanhthu_thuoc + baoCao.tmh.doanhthu_thuthuat + baoCao.kinh.doanhthu) * 100) || 0).toFixed(2)
    : '0';

  return (
    <div className="p-6">
      <Toaster position="top-right" />
      <h1 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Báo Cáo Doanh Thu và Lãi</h1>
      <div className="flex gap-4 mb-4">
        <Input
          type="date"
          value={fromDate}
          onChange={(e) => setFromDate(e.target.value)}
          className="w-40"
        />
        <Input
          type="date"
          value={toDate}
          onChange={(e) => setToDate(e.target.value)}
          className="w-40"
        />
        <select
          value={chuyenKhoa}
          onChange={(e) => setChuyenKhoa(e.target.value)}
          className="border rounded p-2"
        >
          <option value="">Tất cả chuyên khoa</option>
          <option value="Mắt">Mắt</option>
          <option value="TMH">TMH</option>
          <option value="Kính">Kính</option>
        </select>
        <Button onClick={fetchBaoCao}>Lọc</Button>
      </div>

      {baoCao && (
        <div className="mb-4">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Tổng hợp</h2>
          <Card>
            <CardContent className="p-0">
              <table className="min-w-full text-sm">
                <thead className="bg-gray-100 border-b">
                  <tr>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Hạng mục</th>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1 text-right">Doanh thu (nghìn)</th>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1 text-right">Lãi (nghìn)</th>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1 text-right">Nợ (nghìn)</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                  <tr className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-2 py-1">Mắt - Thuốc</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.mat.doanhthu_thuoc / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.mat.lai_thuoc / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.mat.no_thuoc / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-2 py-1">Mắt - Thủ thuật</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.mat.doanhthu_thuthuat / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.mat.lai_thuthuat / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.mat.no_thuthuat / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-2 py-1">TMH - Thuốc</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.tmh.doanhthu_thuoc / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.tmh.lai_thuoc / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.tmh.no_thuoc / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-2 py-1">TMH - Thủ thuật</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.tmh.doanhthu_thuthuat / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.tmh.lai_thuthuat / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.tmh.no_thuthuat / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-2 py-1">Kính</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.kinh.doanhthu / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.kinh.lai / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(baoCao.kinh.no / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 font-semibold">
                    <td className="px-2 py-1">Tổng tỷ lệ lãi</td>
                    <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right" colSpan={3}>{tongTyLeLai}%</td>
                  </tr>
                </tbody>
              </table>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        </div>
      )}

      <Card>
        <CardContent className="p-0">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2 px-2 pt-2">Chi tiết</h2>
          <table className="min-w-full text-sm">
            <thead className="bg-gray-100 border-b">
              <tr>
                <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Ngày</th>
                <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Chuyên khoa</th>
                <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Loại</th>
                <th className="px-2 py-1 text-right">Doanh thu (nghìn)</th>
                <th className="px-2 py-1 text-right">Lãi (nghìn)</th>
                <th className="px-2 py-1 text-right">Nợ (nghìn)</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {paginated.map((item) => (
                <tr key={`${item.chuyen_khoa}-${item.type}-${item.id}`} className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
                  <td className="px-2 py-1">{new Date(item.ngay).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')}</td>
                  <td className="px-2 py-1">{item.chuyen_khoa}</td>
                  <td className="px-2 py-1">{item.type}</td>
                  <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(item.doanhthu / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                  <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(item.lai / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                  <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(item.no / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                </tr>
              ))}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      <div className="flex justify-center gap-1 mt-2">
        {[...Array(totalPages)].map((_, i) => (
          <button
            key={i + 1}
            onClick={() => setCurrentPage(i + 1)}
            className={`px-2 py-1 border rounded text-sm ${currentPage === i + 1 ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'hover:bg-blue-100'}`}
          >
            {i + 1}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {doanhThuChartData && (
        <div className="mt-4">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Biểu đồ tỷ lệ doanh thu</h2>
          <div className="max-w-md mx-auto">
            <Pie
              data={doanhThuChartData}
              options={{
                plugins: {
                  legend: {
                    position: 'top',
                  },
                  tooltip: {
                    callbacks: {
                      label: (context) => `${context.label}: ${context.parsed.toFixed(0)}k`,
                    },
                  },
                },
              }}
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {laiChartData && (
        <div className="mt-4">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Biểu đồ tổng lãi theo ngày</h2>
          <Bar
            data={laiChartData}
            options={{
              scales: {
                y: {
                  beginAtZero: true,
                  title: { display: true, text: 'Tổng lãi (nghìn)' },
                },
                x: {
                  title: { display: true, text: 'Ngày' },
                },
              },
              plugins: {
                legend: {
                  display: false,
                },
                tooltip: {
                  callbacks: {
                    label: (context) => `Tổng lãi: ${context.parsed.y.toFixed(0)}k`,
                  },
                },
              },
            }}
          />
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

import { Routes, Route } from 'react-router-dom';
import Login from './components/Login.jsx';
import Signup from './components/Signup.jsx';
import ProtectedRoute from './components/ProtectedRoute.jsx';

function App() {
  return (
    <div className="container mx-auto p-4">
      <Routes>
        <Route path="/login" element={<Login />} />
        <Route path="/signup" element={<Signup />} />
        <Route
          path="/"
          element={
            <ProtectedRoute>
              <h1>Trang quản lý bệnh nhân</h1>
            </ProtectedRoute>
          }
        />
      </Routes>
    </div>
  );
}

export default App;

## File: src\components\ke-don\QuaTrinhDieuTri.tsx

```tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from "react"
import { getDonThuocByBenhNhan } from "@/lib/api/thuoc"
import { DonThuoc } from "@prisma/client"
import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area"
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle } from "@/components/ui/dialog"

interface QuaTrinhDieuTriProps {
  benhNhanId: string
}

export default function QuaTrinhDieuTri({ benhNhanId }: QuaTrinhDieuTriProps) {
  const [donThuocList, setDonThuocList] = useState<DonThuoc[]>([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
  const [donXemLai, setDonXemLai] = useState<DonThuoc | null>(null)
  const [openDialog, setOpenDialog] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => {
    async function fetchData() {
      setLoading(true)
      const data = await getDonThuocByBenhNhan(benhNhanId)
      setDonThuocList(data || [])
      setLoading(false)
    }
    if (benhNhanId) fetchData()
  }, [benhNhanId])

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
      <div className="font-semibold text-sm mb-2">Quá trình điều trị</div>
      <ScrollArea className="flex-1 border rounded-md">
        {loading ? (
          <div className="p-4 text-sm text-muted-foreground">Đang tải...</div>
        ) : donThuocList.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="p-4 text-sm text-muted-foreground">Chưa có đơn thuốc</div>
        ) : (
          <div className="p-2 space-y-1">
            {donThuocList.map((don) => (
              <div
                key={don.id}
                className="cursor-pointer hover:bg-muted p-2 rounded"
                onClick={() => {
                  setDonXemLai(don)
                  setOpenDialog(true)
                }}
              >
                <div className="text-sm font-medium">
                  {new Date(don.ngay).toLocaleDateString("vi-VN")}
                </div>
                <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                  {don.chanDoan || "Không có chẩn đoán"}
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </ScrollArea>

      <Dialog open={openDialog} onOpenChange={(open) => {
        setOpenDialog(open)
        if (!open) setDonXemLai(null)
      }}>
        <DialogContent className="max-w-xl">
          <DialogHeader>
            <DialogTitle>Đơn thuốc ngày {donXemLai && new Date(donXemLai.ngay).toLocaleDateString("vi-VN")}</DialogTitle>
          </DialogHeader>
          {donXemLai && (
            <div className="space-y-2 text-sm">
              <div><strong>Chẩn đoán:</strong> {donXemLai.chanDoan || "Không có"}</div>
              <div><strong>Diễn tiến:</strong> {donXemLai.dienTien || "Không có"}</div>
              <div>
                <strong>Danh sách thuốc:</strong>
                <ul className="list-disc pl-5 mt-1">
                  {donXemLai.thuoc?.map((t, i) => (
                    <li key={i}>
                      {t.ten} - {t.lieuDung} - SL: {t.soLuong} {t.ghiChu ? `(${t.ghiChu})` : ""}
                    </li>
                  )) || <li>Không có thuốc</li>}
                </ul>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </DialogContent>
      </Dialog>
    </div>
  )
}

```

## File: src\components\Login.jsx

```jsx
import { useState } from 'react';
import { supabase } from '../supabase';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

function Login() {
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const handleLogin = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
        email,
        password,
      });
      if (error) throw error;
      alert('Đăng nhập thành công!');
      navigate('/');
    } catch (error) {
      setError(error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleGoogleLogin = async () => {
    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOAuth({
        provider: 'google',
      });
      if (error) throw error;
    } catch (error) {
      setError(error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="max-w-md mx-auto">
      <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Đăng nhập</h2>
      <form onSubmit={handleLogin} className="space-y-4">
        <input
          type="email"
          placeholder="Email"
          value={email}
          onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded"
        />
        <input
          type="password"
          placeholder="Mật khẩu"
          value={password}
          onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded"
        />
        <button type="submit" className="w-full p-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded">
          Đăng nhập
        </button>
      </form>
      <button
        onClick={handleGoogleLogin}
        className="w-full p-2 mt-2 bg-red-500 text-white rounded"
      >
        Đăng nhập với Google
      </button>
      {error && <p className="text-red-500 mt-2">{error}</p>}
    </div>
  );
}

export default Login;
```

## File: src\components\ProtectedRoute.jsx

```jsx
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { supabase } from '../supabase';

function ProtectedRoute({ children }) {
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  useEffect(() => {
    const checkSession = async () => {
      const { data: { session } } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
      if (!session) {
        navigate('/login');
      }
    };
    checkSession();
  }, [navigate]);

  return children;
}

export default ProtectedRoute;
```

```jsx
import { useState } from 'react';
import { supabase } from '../supabase';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

function Signup() {
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const handleSignup = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
        email,
        password,
      });
      if (error) throw error;
      alert('Đăng ký thành công! Vui lòng kiểm tra email để xác nhận.');
      navigate('/login');
    } catch (error) {
      setError(error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="max-w-md mx-auto">
      <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Đăng ký</h2>
      <form onSubmit={handleSignup} className="space-y-4">
        <input
          type="email"
          placeholder="Email"
          value={email}
          onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded"
        />
        <input
          type="password"
          placeholder="Mật khẩu"
          value={password}
          onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded"
        />
        <button type="submit" className="w-full p-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded">
          Đăng ký
        </button>
      </form>
      {error && <p className="text-red-500 mt-2">{error}</p>}
    </div>
  );
}

export default Signup;

## File: src\components\ui\button.tsx

```tsx
import * as React from "react"
import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const buttonVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default:
          "bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-xs hover:bg-primary/90",
        destructive:
          "bg-destructive text-white shadow-xs hover:bg-destructive/90 focus-visible:ring-destructive/20 dark:focus-visible:ring-destructive/40 dark:bg-destructive/60",
        outline:
          "border bg-background shadow-xs hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:bg-input/30 dark:border-input dark:hover:bg-input/50",
        secondary:
          "bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground shadow-xs hover:bg-secondary/80",
        ghost:
          "hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50",
        link: "text-primary underline-offset-4 hover:underline",
      },
      size: {
        default: "h-9 px-4 py-2 has-[>svg]:px-3",
        sm: "h-8 rounded-md gap-1.5 px-3 has-[>svg]:px-2.5",
        lg: "h-10 rounded-md px-6 has-[>svg]:px-4",
        icon: "size-9",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
      size: "default",
    },
  }
)

function Button({
  className,
  variant,
  size,
  asChild = false,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<"button"> &
  VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> & {
    asChild?: boolean
  }) {
  const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button"

  return (
    <Comp
      data-slot="button"
      className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

export { Button, buttonVariants }

```

"use client"

import * as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { XIcon } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

function Dialog({
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Root>) {
  return <DialogPrimitive.Root data-slot="dialog" {...props} />
}

function DialogTrigger({
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Trigger>) {
  return <DialogPrimitive.Trigger data-slot="dialog-trigger" {...props} />

  return <DialogPrimitive.Portal data-slot="dialog-portal" {...props} />

## File: src\components\ui\form.tsx

```tsx
"use client"

import * as React from "react"
import * as LabelPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-label"
import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"
import {
  Controller,
  FormProvider,
  useFormContext,
  useFormState,
  type ControllerProps,
  type FieldPath,
  type FieldValues,
} from "react-hook-form"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label"

const Form = FormProvider

type FormFieldContextValue<
  TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
  TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
> = {
  name: TName
}

const FormFieldContext = React.createContext<FormFieldContextValue>(
  {} as FormFieldContextValue
)

const FormField = <
  TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
  TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
>({
  ...props
}: ControllerProps<TFieldValues, TName>) => {
  return (
    <FormFieldContext.Provider value={{ name: props.name }}>
      <Controller {...props} />
    </FormFieldContext.Provider>
  )
}

const useFormField = () => {
  const fieldContext = React.useContext(FormFieldContext)
  const itemContext = React.useContext(FormItemContext)
  const { getFieldState } = useFormContext()
  const formState = useFormState({ name: fieldContext.name })
  const fieldState = getFieldState(fieldContext.name, formState)

  if (!fieldContext) {
    throw new Error("useFormField should be used within <FormField>")
  }

  const { id } = itemContext

  return {
    id,
    name: fieldContext.name,
    formItemId: `${id}-form-item`,
    formDescriptionId: `${id}-form-item-description`,
    formMessageId: `${id}-form-item-message`,
    ...fieldState,
  }
}

type FormItemContextValue = {
  id: string
}

const FormItemContext = React.createContext<FormItemContextValue>(
  {} as FormItemContextValue
)

function FormItem({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
  const id = React.useId()

  return (
    <FormItemContext.Provider value={{ id }}>
      <div
        data-slot="form-item"
        className={cn("grid gap-2", className)}
        {...props}
      />
    </FormItemContext.Provider>
  )
}

function FormLabel({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<typeof LabelPrimitive.Root>) {
  const { error, formItemId } = useFormField()

  return (
    <Label
      data-slot="form-label"
      data-error={!!error}
      className={cn("data-[error=true]:text-destructive", className)}
      htmlFor={formItemId}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function FormControl({ ...props }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Slot>) {
  const { error, formItemId, formDescriptionId, formMessageId } = useFormField()

  return (
    <Slot
      data-slot="form-control"
      id={formItemId}
      aria-describedby={
        !error
          ? `${formDescriptionId}`
          : `${formDescriptionId} ${formMessageId}`
      }
      aria-invalid={!!error}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function FormDescription({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
  const { formDescriptionId } = useFormField()

  return (
    <p
      data-slot="form-description"
      id={formDescriptionId}
      className={cn("text-muted-foreground text-sm", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function FormMessage({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
  const { error, formMessageId } = useFormField()
  const body = error ? String(error?.message ?? "") : props.children

  if (!body) {
    return null
  }

  return (
    <p
      data-slot="form-message"
      id={formMessageId}
      className={cn("text-destructive text-sm", className)}
      {...props}
    >
      {body}
    </p>
  )
}

export {
  useFormField,
  Form,
  FormItem,
  FormLabel,
  FormControl,
  FormDescription,
  FormMessage,
  FormField,
}

```

  TableBody,
  TableFooter,
  TableHead,
  TableRow,
  TableCell,
  TableCaption,
}

## File: src\lib\queryClient.ts

```ts
// lib/queryClient.ts
import { QueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';

export const queryClient = new QueryClient({
  defaultOptions: {
    queries: {
      // Thời gian cache dữ liệu (mặc định 5 phút)
      staleTime: 1000 * 60 * 5, // 5 phút
      // Thời gian giữ cache khi không sử dụng (mặc định 5 phút)
      cacheTime: 1000 * 60 * 5, // 5 phút
      // Tự động refetch khi window focus (mặc định true)
      refetchOnWindowFocus: false, // Tắt để tiết kiệm tài nguyên
      // Số lần thử lại khi truy vấn thất bại
      retry: 2,
      // Thời gian chờ trước khi thử lại (ms)
      retryDelay: (attempt) => Math.min(1000 * 2 ** attempt, 30000),
    },
    mutations: {
      // Số lần thử lại khi mutation thất bại
      retry: 1,
    },
  },
});

## File: src\pages\api\bao-cao\index.ts

```ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from 'next';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  if (req.method !== 'GET') {
    return res.status(405).json({ message: `Phương thức ${req.method} không được hỗ trợ` });
  }

  const { from, to, chuyen_khoa } = req.query;

  if (!from || !to) {
    return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Thiếu tham số from hoặc to' });
  }

  try {
    // Lấy đơn thuốc
    let queryThuoc = supabase
      .from('DonThuoc')
      .select('id, ngaylap, tongtien, sotien_da_thanh_toan, chuyen_khoa')
      .gte('ngaylap', from as string)
      .lte('ngaylap', to as string);

    if (chuyen_khoa) {
      queryThuoc = queryThuoc.eq('chuyen_khoa', chuyen_khoa as string);
    }

    const { data: donThuocs, error: errorThuoc } = await queryThuoc;
    if (errorThuoc) {
      console.error('Lỗi truy vấn DonThuoc:', errorThuoc);
      throw new Error(`Lỗi truy vấn DonThuoc: ${errorThuoc.message}`);
    }

    // Lấy chi tiết đơn thuốc và thông tin thuốc
    const donThuocIds = donThuocs.map((don) => don.id);
    const { data: chiTietThuocs, error: errorChiTiet } = await supabase
      .from('ChiTietDonThuoc')
      .select('donthuocid, soluong, thuoc:thuocid(giaban, gianhap, donvitinh)')
      .in('donthuocid', donThuocIds);

    if (errorChiTiet) {
      console.error('Lỗi truy vấn ChiTietDonThuoc:', errorChiTiet);
      throw new Error(`Lỗi truy vấn ChiTietDonThuoc: ${errorChiTiet.message}`);
    }

    // Lấy đơn kính
    let queryKinh = supabase
      .from('DonKinh')
      .select('id, ngaykham, giatrong, giagong, sotienno, lai')
      .gte('ngaykham', from as string)
      .lte('ngaykham', to as string);

    const { data: donKinhs, error: errorKinh } = await queryKinh;
    if (errorKinh) {
      console.error('Lỗi truy vấn DonKinh:', errorKinh);
      throw new Error(`Lỗi truy vấn DonKinh: ${errorKinh.message}`);
    }

    // Tổng hợp dữ liệu
    const baoCao = {
      mat: {
        doanhthu_thuoc: 0,
        doanhthu_thuthuat: 0,
        lai_thuoc: 0,
        lai_thuthuat: 0,
        no_thuoc: 0,
        no_thuthuat: 0,
      },
      tmh: {
        doanhthu_thuoc: 0,
        doanhthu_thuthuat: 0,
        lai_thuoc: 0,
        lai_thuthuat: 0,
        no_thuoc: 0,
        no_thuthuat: 0,
      },
      kinh: {
        doanhthu: donKinhs.reduce((sum, don) => sum + (don.giatrong || 0) + (don.giagong || 0), 0),
        lai: donKinhs.reduce((sum, don) => sum + (don.lai || 0), 0),
        no: donKinhs.reduce((sum, don) => sum + (don.sotienno || 0), 0),
      },
      chi_tiet: {
        mat: { thuoc: [], thuthuat: [] },
        tmh: { thuoc: [], thuthuat: [] },
        kinh: [],
      },
    };

    // Xử lý thuốc và thủ thuật
    donThuocs.forEach((don) => {
      const chuyenKhoa = don.chuyen_khoa === 'Mắt' ? 'mat' : 'tmh';
      const chiTiets = chiTietThuocs.filter((ct) => ct.donthuocid === don.id);
      const doanhthuThuoc = chiTiets
        .filter((ct) => ct.thuoc.donvitinh !== 'lần')
        .reduce((sum, ct) => sum + ct.soluong * ct.thuoc.giaban, 0);
      const doanhthuThuthuat = chiTiets
        .filter((ct) => ct.thuoc.donvitinh === 'lần')
        .reduce((sum, ct) => sum + ct.soluong * ct.thuoc.giaban, 0);
      const laiThuoc = chiTiets
        .filter((ct) => ct.thuoc.donvitinh !== 'lần')
        .reduce((sum, ct) => sum + ct.soluong * (ct.thuoc.giaban - (ct.thuoc.gianhap || 0)), 0);
      const laiThuthuat = chiTiets
        .filter((ct) => ct.thuoc.donvitinh === 'lần')
        .reduce((sum, ct) => sum + ct.soluong * (ct.thuoc.giaban - (ct.thuoc.gianhap || 0)), 0);
      const no = don.tongtien - (don.sotien_da_thanh_toan || 0);
      const noThuoc = don.tongtien ? (doanhthuThuoc / don.tongtien) * no : 0;
      const noThuthuat = don.tongtien ? (doanhthuThuthuat / don.tongtien) * no : 0;

      baoCao[chuyenKhoa].doanhthu_thuoc += doanhthuThuoc;
      baoCao[chuyenKhoa].doanhthu_thuthuat += doanhthuThuthuat;
      baoCao[chuyenKhoa].lai_thuoc += laiThuoc;
      baoCao[chuyenKhoa].lai_thuthuat += laiThuthuat;
      baoCao[chuyenKhoa].no_thuoc += noThuoc;
      baoCao[chuyenKhoa].no_thuthuat += noThuthuat;

      if (doanhthuThuoc > 0) {
        baoCao.chi_tiet[chuyenKhoa].thuoc.push({
          id: don.id,
          ngay: don.ngaylap,
          doanhthu: doanhthuThuoc,
          lai: laiThuoc,
          no: noThuoc,
        });
      }
      if (doanhthuThuthuat > 0) {
        baoCao.chi_tiet[chuyenKhoa].thuthuat.push({
          id: don.id,
          ngay: don.ngaylap,
          doanhthu: doanhthuThuthuat,
          lai: laiThuthuat,
          no: noThuthuat,
        });
      }
    });

    // Xử lý chi tiết kính
    baoCao.chi_tiet.kinh = donKinhs.map((don) => ({
      id: don.id,
      ngay: don.ngaykham,
      doanhthu: (don.giatrong || 0) + (don.giagong || 0),
      lai: don.lai || 0,
      no: don.sotienno || 0,
    }));

    return res.status(200).json({ data: baoCao });
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error('Lỗi trong API bao-cao:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ message: 'Lỗi server', error: error.message });
  }
}
```

## File: src\pages\api\benh-nhan\index.ts

```ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from "next";
import { createClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";

// Định nghĩa interface cho dữ liệu bệnh nhân
interface BenhNhan {
  id: number;
  mabenhnhan: string;
  ten: string;
  namsinh: number;
  gioitinh: string;
  dienthoai: string;
  diachi: string;
}

// Định nghĩa interface cho lỗi Supabase
interface SupabaseError {
  message: string;
  code?: string;
  details?: string;
  hint?: string;
}

// Initialize Supabase client
const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
  {
    global: {
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}`,
      },
    },
  }
);

export default async function handler(
  req: NextApiRequest,
  res: NextApiResponse<BenhNhan | BenhNhan[] | { message: string; error?: string }>
) {
  // Handle GET requests
  if (req.method === "GET") {
    try {
      const benhnhanid = req.query.benhnhanid as string;
      const page = parseInt(req.query.page as string) || 1;
      const pageSize = parseInt(req.query.pageSize as string) || 100;
      const search = (req.query.search as string)?.toLowerCase() || "";
      const from = (page - 1) * pageSize;
      const to = from + pageSize - 1;

      if (benhnhanid) {
        // Fetch a specific patient
        const { data, error } = await supabase
          .from("BenhNhan")
          .select("id, mabenhnhan, ten, namsinh, gioitinh, dienthoai, diachi")
          .eq("id", benhnhanid)
          .single();

        if (error) {
          return res.status(400).json({ message: "Error fetching patient", error: error.message });
        }
        if (!data) {
          return res.status(404).json({ message: "Patient not found" });
        }
        return res.status(200).json({ data });
      } else {
        // Fetch patient list with pagination and search
        let query = supabase
          .from("BenhNhan")
          .select("id, mabenhnhan, ten, namsinh, gioitinh, dienthoai, diachi", { count: "exact" })
          .order("id", { ascending: false });

        if (search) {
          query = query.or(`ten.ilike.%${search}%,mabenhnhan.ilike.%${search}%`);
        }

        const { data, error, count } = await query.range(from, to);

        if (error) {
          return res.status(400).json({ message: "Error fetching patient list", error: error.message });
        }

        return res.status(200).json({ data: data || [], total: count || 0 });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown error";
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Server error", error: message });
    }
  }

  // Handle POST requests
  if (req.method === "POST") {
    try {
      const { mabenhnhan, ten, namsinh, gioitinh, dienthoai, diachi } = req.body;

      if (!ten || !namsinh || !diachi) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Name, birth year, and address are required" });
      }

      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from("BenhNhan")
        .insert([{ mabenhnhan, ten, namsinh, gioitinh, dienthoai, diachi }])
        .select()
        .single();

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Error adding patient", error: error.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ message: "Patient added successfully", data });
    } catch (error) {
      const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown error";
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Server error", error: message });
    }
  }

  // Handle PUT requests
  if (req.method === "PUT") {
    try {
      const { id, mabenhnhan, ten, namsinh, gioitinh, dienthoai, diachi } = req.body;

      if (!id || !ten || !namsinh || !diachi) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "ID, name, birth year, and address are required" });
      }

      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from("BenhNhan")
        .update({ mabenhnhan, ten, namsinh, gioitinh, dienthoai, diachi })
        .eq("id", id)
        .select()
        .single();

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Error updating patient", error: error.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ message: "Patient updated successfully", data });
    } catch (error) {
      const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown error";
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Server error", error: message });
    }
  }

  // Handle DELETE requests
  if (req.method === "DELETE") {
    try {
      const id = req.query.id;

      if (!id) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Patient ID is required" });
      }

      const { error } = await supabase
        .from("BenhNhan")
        .delete()
        .eq("id", id);

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Error deleting patient", error: error.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ message: "Patient deleted successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown error";
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Server error", error: message });
    }
  }

  return res.status(405).json({ message: `Method ${req.method} not allowed` });
}

```

```ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from "next";
import { createClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
  {
    global: {
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}`,
      },
    },
  }
);

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  if (req.method === "GET") {
    try {
      const donthuocid = req.query.donthuocid;

      if (!donthuocid) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Thiếu donthuocid" });
      }

      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from("ChiTietDonThuoc")
        .select(`
          id,
          donthuocid,
          thuocid,
          soluong,
          donvitinh,
          cachdung,
          thuoc:thuocid (
            id,
            tenthuoc,
            donvitinh,
            giaban,
            soluongmacdinh,
            nhomthuoc
          )
        `)
        .eq("donthuocid", donthuocid);

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi lấy chi tiết đơn thuốc", error: error.message });
      }

      if (!data || data.length === 0) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Không tìm thấy chi tiết đơn thuốc" });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ data });
    } catch (error: unknown) {
  const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error);
  return res.status(500).json({ message: "Lỗi server", error: message });
}

  }

  return res.status(405).json({ message: `Phương thức ${req.method} không được hỗ trợ` });
}

      .from('ChoKham')

      .eq('trangthai', 'chờ')
      .order('thoigian', { ascending: true });

## File: src\pages\api\dien-tien\index.ts

```ts
// pages/api/dien-tien/index.ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from "next";
import { createClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
  {
    global: {
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}`,
      },
    },
  }
);

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  const { method } = req;

  if (method === "GET") {
    const benhnhanid = req.query.benhnhanid;
    if (!benhnhanid) {
      return res.status(400).json({ message: "Thiếu ID bệnh nhân" });
    }

    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from("DienTien")
        .select("id, ngay, noidung")
        .eq("benhnhanid", benhnhanid)
        .order("ngay", { ascending: false });

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi truy vấn diễn tiến", error: error.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ data });
    } catch (error: any) {
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Lỗi server", error: error.message });
    }
  }

  if (method === "POST") {
    const { benhnhanid, noidung, ngay } = req.body;

    if (!benhnhanid || !noidung) {
      return res.status(400).json({ message: "Thiếu thông tin diễn tiến" });
    }

    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from("DienTien")
        .insert([{ benhnhanid, noidung, ngay: ngay || new Date().toISOString() }])
        .select()
        .single();

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi thêm diễn tiến", error: error.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ message: "Đã thêm diễn tiến", data });
    } catch (error: any) {
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Lỗi server", error: error.message });
    }
  }

  if (method === "PUT") {
    const { id, noidung, ngay } = req.body;

    if (!id || !noidung) {
      return res.status(400).json({ message: "Thiếu thông tin để sửa diễn tiến" });
    }

    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from("DienTien")
        .update({ noidung, ngay: ngay || new Date().toISOString() })
        .eq("id", id)
        .select()
        .single();

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi sửa diễn tiến", error: error.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ message: "Đã sửa diễn tiến", data });
    } catch (error: any) {
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Lỗi server", error: error.message });
    }
  }

  if (method === "DELETE") {
    const { id } = req.query;

    if (!id) {
      return res.status(400).json({ message: "Thiếu ID diễn tiến" });
    }

    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.from("DienTien").delete().eq("id", id);

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi xoá diễn tiến", error: error.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ message: "Đã xoá diễn tiến" });
    } catch (error: any) {
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Lỗi server", error: error.message });
    }
  }

  return res.status(405).json({ message: `Phương thức ${method} không được hỗ trợ` });
}
```

## File: src\pages\api\don-kinh\index.ts

```ts
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from 'next';

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
  {
    global: {
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}`,
      },
    },
  }
);

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  if (req.method === 'GET') {
    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('DonKinh')
        .select(`*, benhnhan:BenhNhan(id, ten, namsinh, dienthoai)`);
      if (error) throw error;
      res.status(200).json({ data });
    } catch (error: any) {
      console.error('Supabase GET error:', error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: 'Lỗi khi lấy dữ liệu đơn kính', details: error.message });
    }
  } else if (req.method === 'POST') {
    try {
      const {
        benhnhanid,
        chandoan,
        ngaykham,
        giatrong,
        giagong,
        ghichu,
        thiluc_khongkinh_mp,
        thiluc_kinhcu_mp,
        thiluc_kinhmoi_mp,
        sokinh_cu_mp,
        sokinh_moi_mp,
        hangtrong_mp,
        ax_mp,
        thiluc_khongkinh_mt,
        thiluc_kinhcu_mt,
        thiluc_kinhmoi_mt,
        sokinh_cu_mt,
        sokinh_moi_mt,
        hangtrong_mt,
        ax_mt,
        no,
        sotienno,
        lai,
      } = req.body;

      if (!benhnhanid || !chandoan || !ngaykham) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Thiếu thông tin bắt buộc' });
      }

      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('DonKinh')
        .insert([
          {
            benhnhanid,
            chandoan,
            ngaykham,
            giatrong,
            giagong,
            ghichu: ghichu || '',
            thiluc_khongkinh_mp: thiluc_khongkinh_mp || '',
            thiluc_kinhcu_mp: thiluc_kinhcu_mp || '',
            thiluc_kinhmoi_mp: thiluc_kinhmoi_mp || '',
            sokinh_cu_mp: sokinh_cu_mp || '',
            sokinh_moi_mp: sokinh_moi_mp || '',
            hangtrong_mp: hangtrong_mp || '',
            ax_mp,
            thiluc_khongkinh_mt: thiluc_khongkinh_mt || '',
            thiluc_kinhcu_mt: thiluc_kinhcu_mt || '',
            thiluc_kinhmoi_mt: thiluc_kinhmoi_mt || '',
            sokinh_cu_mt: sokinh_cu_mt || '',
            sokinh_moi_mt: sokinh_moi_mt || '',
            hangtrong_mt: hangtrong_mt || '',
            ax_mt,
            no: no || false,
            sotienno: sotienno || 0,
            lai: lai || 0,
          },
        ])
        .select(`*, benhnhan:BenhNhan(id, ten, namsinh, dienthoai)`).maybeSingle();

      if (error) throw error;
      res.status(200).json({ data });
    } catch (error: any) {
      console.error('Supabase POST error:', error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: 'Lỗi khi tạo đơn kính', details: error.message });
    }
  } else if (req.method === 'PUT') {
    try {
      const {
        id,
        benhnhanid,
        chandoan,
        ngaykham,
        giatrong,
        giagong,
        ghichu,
        thiluc_khongkinh_mp,
        thiluc_kinhcu_mp,
        thiluc_kinhmoi_mp,
        sokinh_cu_mp,
        sokinh_moi_mp,
        hangtrong_mp,
        ax_mp,
        thiluc_khongkinh_mt,
        thiluc_kinhcu_mt,
        thiluc_kinhmoi_mt,
        sokinh_cu_mt,
        sokinh_moi_mt,
        hangtrong_mt,
        ax_mt,
        no,
        sotienno,
        lai,
      } = req.body;

      if (!id || !benhnhanid || !chandoan || !ngaykham) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Thiếu thông tin bắt buộc để cập nhật' });
      }

      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('DonKinh')
        .update({
          benhnhanid,
          chandoan,
          ngaykham,
          giatrong,
          giagong,
          ghichu: ghichu || '',
          thiluc_khongkinh_mp: thiluc_khongkinh_mp || '',
          thiluc_kinhcu_mp: thiluc_kinhcu_mp || '',
          thiluc_kinhmoi_mp: thiluc_kinhmoi_mp || '',
          sokinh_cu_mp: sokinh_cu_mp || '',
          sokinh_moi_mp: sokinh_moi_mp || '',
          hangtrong_mp: hangtrong_mp || '',
          ax_mp,
          thiluc_khongkinh_mt: thiluc_khongkinh_mt || '',
          thiluc_kinhcu_mt: thiluc_kinhcu_mt || '',
          thiluc_kinhmoi_mt: thiluc_kinhmoi_mt || '',
          sokinh_cu_mt: sokinh_cu_mt || '',
          sokinh_moi_mt: sokinh_moi_mt || '',
          hangtrong_mt: hangtrong_mt || '',
          ax_mt,
          no: no || false,
          sotienno: sotienno || 0,
          lai: lai || 0,
        })
        .eq('id', id)
        .select(`*, benhnhan:BenhNhan(id, ten, namsinh, dienthoai)`).maybeSingle();

      if (error) throw error;
      res.status(200).json({ data });
    } catch (error: any) {
      console.error('Supabase PUT error:', error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: 'Lỗi khi cập nhật đơn kính', details: error.message });
    }
  } else if (req.method === 'DELETE') {
    try {
      const { id } = req.query;

      if (!id) return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Thiếu ID để xoá đơn kính' });

      const { error } = await supabase.from('DonKinh').delete().eq('id', Number(id));
      if (error) throw error;

      res.status(200).json({ message: 'Đã xoá đơn kính' });
    } catch (error: any) {
      console.error('Supabase DELETE error:', error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: 'Lỗi khi xoá đơn kính', details: error.message });
    }
  } else {
    res.setHeader('Allow', ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE']);
    res.status(405).json({ message: `Phương thức ${req.method} không được phép` });
  }
}

## File: src\pages\api\don-thuoc\index.ts

```ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from "next";
import { createClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
  {
    global: {
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}`,
      },
    },
  }
);

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  if (req.method === "GET") {
    try {
      const { benhnhanid } = req.query;

      let query = supabase
        .from("DonThuoc")
        .select(`
          id,
          madonthuoc,
          chandoan,
          chuyen_khoa,
          ngaylap,
          tongtien,
          trangthai_thanh_toan,
          sotien_da_thanh_toan,
          benhnhan:BenhNhan(id, ten, namsinh, dienthoai, diachi)
        `)
        .order("ngaylap", { ascending: false });

      if (benhnhanid) {
        query = query.eq("benhnhanid", benhnhanid);
      }

      const { data, error } = await query;

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi lấy đơn thuốc", error: error.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ data });
    } catch (error: any) {
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Lỗi server", error: error.message });
    }
  }

  if (req.method === "POST") {
    try {
      const { benhnhanid, chandoan, chuyen_khoa, thuocs, sotien_da_thanh_toan } = req.body;

      if (!benhnhanid || !chandoan || !thuocs || thuocs.length === 0) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Thiếu thông tin bắt buộc" });
      }

      // Validate thuocs
      for (const t of thuocs) {
        if (!t.id || !Number.isInteger(t.soluong) || t.soluong <= 0) {
          return res.status(400).json({ message: "Dữ liệu thuốc không hợp lệ", details: `thuocid: ${t.id}, soluong: ${t.soluong}` });
        }
      }

      const tongtien = thuocs.reduce((sum: number, t: any) => sum + t.soluong * t.giaban, 0);
      const trangthai_thanh_toan = sotien_da_thanh_toan >= tongtien ? 'đã thanh toán' : 'nợ';

      const { data: donthuoc, error: donthuocError } = await supabase
        .from("DonThuoc")
        .insert([
          {
            benhnhanid,
            chandoan,
            chuyen_khoa,
            tongtien,
            trangthai_thanh_toan,
            sotien_da_thanh_toan: sotien_da_thanh_toan || 0,
            madonthuoc: `DT${Date.now().toString().slice(-6)}`,
            ngaylap: new Date().toISOString(),
          },
        ])
        .select(`
          id,
          madonthuoc,
          chandoan,
          chuyen_khoa,
          ngaylap,
          tongtien,
          trangthai_thanh_toan,
          sotien_da_thanh_toan,
          benhnhan:BenhNhan(id, ten, namsinh, dienthoai, diachi)
        `)
        .single();

      if (donthuocError) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi tạo đơn thuốc", error: donthuocError.message });
      }

      const chiTietInserts = thuocs.map((t: any) => ({
        donthuocid: donthuoc.id,
        thuocid: t.id,
        soluong: t.soluong,
        donvitinh: t.donvitinh,
        cachdung: t.cachdung,
      }));

      const { error: chiTietError } = await supabase
        .from("ChiTietDonThuoc")
        .insert(chiTietInserts);

      if (chiTietError) {
        await supabase.from("DonThuoc").delete().eq("id", donthuoc.id);
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi tạo chi tiết đơn thuốc", error: chiTietError.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ message: "Đã tạo đơn thuốc", data: donthuoc });
    } catch (error: any) {
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Lỗi server", error: error.message });
    }
  }

  if (req.method === "PUT") {
    try {
      const { id, benhnhanid, chandoan, chuyen_khoa, thuocs, sotien_da_thanh_toan } = req.body;

      if (!id || !benhnhanid || !chandoan || !thuocs || thuocs.length === 0) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Thiếu thông tin bắt buộc" });
      }

      // Validate thuocs
      for (const t of thuocs) {
        if (!t.id || !Number.isInteger(t.soluong) || t.soluong <= 0) {
          return res.status(400).json({ message: "Dữ liệu thuốc không hợp lệ", details: `thuocid: ${t.id}, soluong: ${t.soluong}` });
        }
      }

      const tongtien = thuocs.reduce((sum: number, t: any) => sum + t.soluong * t.giaban, 0);
      const trangthai_thanh_toan = sotien_da_thanh_toan >= tongtien ? 'đã thanh toán' : 'nợ';

      const { data: donthuoc, error: donthuocError } = await supabase
        .from("DonThuoc")
        .update({
          chandoan,
          chuyen_khoa,
          tongtien,
          trangthai_thanh_toan,
          sotien_da_thanh_toan: sotien_da_thanh_toan || 0,
        })
        .eq("id", id)
        .select(`
          id,
          madonthuoc,
          chandoan,
          chuyen_khoa,
          ngaylap,
          tongtien,
          trangthai_thanh_toan,
          sotien_da_thanh_toan,
          benhnhan:BenhNhan(id, ten, namsinh, dienthoai, diachi)
        `)
        .single();

      if (donthuocError) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi cập nhật đơn thuốc", error: donthuocError.message });
      }

      await supabase.from("ChiTietDonThuoc").delete().eq("donthuocid", id);

      const chiTietInserts = thuocs.map((t: any) => ({
        donthuocid: id,
        thuocid: t.id,
        soluong: t.soluong,
        donvitinh: t.donvitinh,
        cachdung: t.cachdung,
      }));

      const { error: chiTietError } = await supabase
        .from("ChiTietDonThuoc")
        .insert(chiTietInserts);

      if (chiTietError) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi cập nhật chi tiết đơn thuốc", error: chiTietError.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ message: "Đã cập nhật đơn thuốc", data: donthuoc });
    } catch (error: any) {
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Lỗi server", error: error.message });
    }
  }

  if (req.method === "DELETE") {
    try {
      const id = req.query.id;

      if (!id) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Thiếu ID đơn thuốc" });
      }

      await supabase.from("ChiTietDonThuoc").delete().eq("donthuocid", id);
      const { error } = await supabase.from("DonThuoc").delete().eq("id", id);

      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Lỗi khi xóa đơn thuốc", error: error.message });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({ message: "Đã xóa đơn thuốc" });
    } catch (error: any) {
      return res.status(500).json({ message: "Lỗi server", error: error.message });
    }
  }

  return res.status(405).json({ message: `Phương thức ${req.method} không được hỗ trợ` });
}
