## File: src\pages\api\ke-don\index.ts

```ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from 'next';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
  {
    global: {
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}`,
      },
    },
  }
);

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  if (req.method !== 'POST') {
    return res.status(405).json({ message: `Phương thức ${req.method} không được hỗ trợ` });
  }

  try {
    const { benhnhanid, chandoan, chuyen_khoa, thuocs, trangthai_thanh_toan } = req.body;

    if (!benhnhanid || !chandoan || !chuyen_khoa || !thuocs || !Array.isArray(thuocs)) {
      return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Thiếu hoặc dữ liệu không hợp lệ' });
    }

    const tongtien = thuocs.reduce((sum: number, t: any) => sum + t.soluong * t.giaban, 0);

    const newDonThuoc = {
      madonthuoc: `DT${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7).toUpperCase()}`,
      benhnhanid,
      chandoan,
      chuyen_khoa,
      ngaylap: new Date().toISOString(),
      tongtien,
      trangthai_thanh_toan: trangthai_thanh_toan || 'đã thanh toán',
    };

    const { data: newDonThuocData, error: insertDonThuocError } = await supabase
      .from('DonThuoc')
      .insert(newDonThuoc)
      .select('id, madonthuoc, benhnhanid, chandoan, chuyen_khoa, ngaylap, tongtien, trangthai_thanh_toan')
      .single();

    if (insertDonThuocError || !newDonThuocData) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        message: 'Lỗi khi tạo đơn thuốc mới',
        error: insertDonThuocError?.message,
        details: insertDonThuocError?.details,
      });
    }

    const chiTietToInsert = thuocs.map((t: any) => ({
      donthuocid: newDonThuocData.id,
      thuocid: t.id,
      soluong: t.soluong,
      donvitinh: t.donvitinh,
      cachdung: t.cachdung,
    }));

    const { error: insertChiTietError } = await supabase
      .from('ChiTietDonThuoc')
      .insert(chiTietToInsert);

    if (insertChiTietError) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        message: 'Lỗi khi tạo chi tiết đơn thuốc mới',
        error: insertChiTietError.message,
        details: insertChiTietError.details,
      });
    }

    if (trangthai_thanh_toan === 'nợ') {
      const trangThaiNo = 'chưa trả';
      const { error: insertNoError } = await supabase
        .from('NoBenhNhan')
        .insert({
          benhnhanid,
          donthuocid: newDonThuocData.id,
          sotienno: tongtien,
          ngayno: new Date().toISOString(),
          trangthai: trangThaiNo,
          sotientra: 0,
        });

      if (insertNoError) {
        return res.status(400).json({
          message: 'Lỗi khi ghi nợ',
          error: insertNoError.message,
          details: insertNoError.details,
        });
      }
    }

    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Đã tạo đơn thuốc', data: newDonThuocData });
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error('Server error:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({
      message: 'Lỗi server',
      error: error.message,
      details: error.details || 'Không có chi tiết lỗi',
    });
  }
}
```

## File: src\pages\api\nhom-thuoc\index.ts

```ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from 'next';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  if (req.method === 'GET') {
    const { data, error } = await supabase.from('NhomThuoc').select('*').order('id');
    if (error) return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Lỗi lấy nhóm thuốc', error: error.message });
    return res.status(200).json({ data });
  }

  else if (req.method === 'POST') {
    const { ten } = req.body;
    if (!ten) return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Thiếu tên nhóm' });

    const { data, error } = await supabase.from('NhomThuoc').insert([{ ten }]).select();
    if (error) return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Lỗi khi thêm', error: error.message });
    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Đã thêm nhóm thuốc', data });
  }

  else if (req.method === 'PUT') {
    const { id, ten } = req.body;
    if (!id || !ten) return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Thiếu thông tin' });

    const { error } = await supabase.from('NhomThuoc').update({ ten }).eq('id', id);
    if (error) return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Cập nhật thất bại', error: error.message });
    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Đã cập nhật nhóm thuốc' });
  }

  else if (req.method === 'DELETE') {
    const id = req.query.id;
    if (!id) return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Thiếu id nhóm' });

    const { error } = await supabase.from('NhomThuoc').delete().eq('id', id);
    if (error) return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Xoá thất bại', error: error.message });
    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Đã xoá nhóm thuốc' });
  }

  else {
    return res.status(405).json({ message: 'Phương thức không được hỗ trợ' });
  }
}

```

## File: src\pages\api\thuoc\index.ts

```ts
// File: /pages/api/thuoc/index.ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from 'next';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  const method = req.method;

  if (method === 'GET') {
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('Thuoc')
      .select('*, nhomthuocs:NhomThuoc(id)')
      .order('id', { ascending: false });
    if (error) return res.status(500).json({ error });

    const parsed = data.map((item: any) => ({
      ...item,
      nhomthuocs: item.nhomthuocs.map((n: any) => n.id),
    }));
    return res.status(200).json({ data: parsed });
  }

  if (method === 'POST') {
    const { nhomthuocs, ...thuoc } = req.body;
    const { data, error } = await supabase.from('Thuoc').insert([thuoc]).select();
    if (error || !data || !data[0]) return res.status(400).json({ error });

    const thuocId = data[0].id;
    for (let nhomId of nhomthuocs || []) {
      await supabase.from('ThuocNhom').insert({ thuocId, nhomId });
    }

    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Đã thêm thuốc', data });
  }

  if (method === 'PUT') {
    const { id, nhomthuocs, ...rest } = req.body;
    const { error } = await supabase.from('Thuoc').update(rest).eq('id', id);
    if (error) return res.status(400).json({ error });

    await supabase.from('ThuocNhom').delete().eq('thuocId', id);
    for (let nhomId of nhomthuocs || []) {
      await supabase.from('ThuocNhom').insert({ thuocId: id, nhomId });
    }

    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Đã cập nhật thuốc' });
  }

  if (method === 'DELETE') {
    const { id } = req.query;
    await supabase.from('ThuocNhom').delete().eq('thuocId', id);
    const { error } = await supabase.from('Thuoc').delete().eq('id', id);
    if (error) return res.status(400).json({ error });
    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Đã xoá thuốc' });
  }

  return res.status(405).json({ message: 'Phương thức không hỗ trợ' });
}

```

## File: src\pages\benh-nhan.tsx

```tsx
"use client";

import React, { useEffect, useState, useCallback, useMemo } from "react";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Card, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card";
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
  DialogFooter,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import { Plus, Pencil, Trash2 } from "lucide-react";
import axios from "axios";
import Link from "next/link";
import toast, { Toaster } from "react-hot-toast";

interface BenhNhan {
  id?: number;
  mabenhnhan: string;
  ten: string;
  namsinh: number;
  gioitinh: string;
  dienthoai: string;
  diachi: string;
}

interface DonThuoc {
  id: number;
  madonthuoc: string;
  chandoan: string;
  chuyenkhoa: string;
  ngaylap: string;
  tongtien: number;
  trangthai_thanh_toan: string;
  sotien_da_thanh_toan: number;
}

interface ChiTietDonThuoc {
  thuoc: {
    id: number;
    tenthuoc: string;
  };
  soluong: number;
}

interface DienTien {
  id: number;
  ngay: string;
  noidung: string;
}

export default function BenhNhanPage() {
  const [benhNhans, setBenhNhans] = useState<BenhNhan[]>([]);
  const [search, setSearch] = useState<string>("");
  const [open, setOpen] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [isEditing, setIsEditing] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [form, setForm] = useState<BenhNhan>({
    mabenhnhan: "",
    ten: "",
    namsinh: 2000,
    gioitinh: "Nam",
    dienthoai: "",
    diachi: "",
  });
  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState<number>(1);
  const [rowsPerPage, setRowsPerPage] = useState<number>(100);
  const [selectedBenhNhanId, setSelectedBenhNhanId] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const [donThuocs, setDonThuocs] = useState<DonThuoc[]>([]);
  const [chiTietDonThuocs, setChiTietDonThuocs] = useState<Record<number, ChiTietDonThuoc[]>>({});
  const [dienTiens, setDienTiens] = useState<Record<number, DienTien[]>>({});
  const [total, setTotal] = useState<number>(0);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchList = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await axios.get(`/api/benh-nhan?page=${currentPage}&pageSize=${rowsPerPage}&search=${search}`);
        setBenhNhans(res.data.data || []);
        setTotal(res.data.total || 0);
      } catch (error: any) {
        toast.error(`Lỗi tải danh sách bệnh nhân: ${error.message}`);
      }
    };
    fetchList();
  }, [currentPage, rowsPerPage, search]);

  const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / rowsPerPage);

  const fetchDonThuoc = useCallback(async (benhnhanid: number): Promise<void> => {
    if (!benhnhanid || isNaN(benhnhanid)) {
      toast.error("Mã bệnh nhân không hợp lệ");
      setDonThuocs([]);
      setChiTietDonThuocs({});
      setDienTiens({});
      return;
    }
    try {
      const resDon = await axios.get(`/api/don-thuoc?benhnhanid=${benhnhanid}`);
      const donThuocs: DonThuoc[] = resDon.data.data || [];
      setDonThuocs(donThuocs);

      const chiTietPromises = donThuocs.map((don) =>
        axios.get(`/api/chi-tiet-don-thuoc?donthuocid=${don.id}`)
      );
      const chiTietResponses = await Promise.all(chiTietPromises);
      const chiTietMap: Record<number, ChiTietDonThuoc[]> = {};
      chiTietResponses.forEach((res, idx) => {
        const donId = donThuocs[idx].id;
        chiTietMap[donId] = res.data.data.map((item: ChiTietDonThuoc) => ({
          thuoc: { id: item.thuoc.id, tenthuoc: item.thuoc.tenthuoc },
          soluong: item.soluong,
        }));
      });
      setChiTietDonThuocs(chiTietMap);

      const resDienTien = await axios.get(`/api/dien-tien?benhnhanid=${benhnhanid}`);
      setDienTiens({ [benhnhanid]: resDienTien.data.data || [] });
    } catch (error: any) {
      toast.error(`Lỗi tải dữ liệu: ${error.response?.data?.message || error.message}`);
      setDonThuocs([]);
      setChiTietDonThuocs({});
      setDienTiens({});
    }
  }, []);

  const handleSelectBenhNhan = useCallback(
    (benhnhanid: number) => {
      if (!benhnhanid || isNaN(benhnhanid)) {
        toast.error('Mã bệnh nhân không hợp lệ');
        return;
      }
      if (selectedBenhNhanId === benhnhanid) {
        setSelectedBenhNhanId(null);
        setDonThuocs([]);
        setChiTietDonThuocs({});
        setDienTiens({});
      } else {
        setSelectedBenhNhanId(benhnhanid);
        fetchDonThuoc(benhnhanid);
      }
    },
    [selectedBenhNhanId, fetchDonThuoc]
  );

  const generateNextMa = useCallback((list: BenhNhan[]) => {
    const max = list.reduce((acc, cur) => {
      const match = cur.mabenhnhan?.match(/BN(\d+)/);
      const num = match ? parseInt(match[1]) : 0;
      return Math.max(acc, num);
    }, 0);
    return `BN${(max + 1).toString().padStart(5, '0')}`;
  }, []);

  const handleSubmit = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!form.ten || !form.namsinh || !form.diachi) {
      toast.error('Họ tên, năm sinh và địa chỉ là bắt buộc!');
      return;
    }
    let finalForm = { ...form };
    if (!isEditing) {
      const nextMa = generateNextMa(benhNhans);
      finalForm.mabenhnhan = finalForm.mabenhnhan.trim() || nextMa;
    }
    try {
      if (isEditing) {
        await axios.put('/api/benh-nhan', finalForm);
        toast.success('Đã cập nhật bệnh nhân');
      } else {
        await axios.post('/api/benh-nhan', finalForm);
        toast.success('Đã thêm bệnh nhân');
      }
      setOpen(false);
      const res = await axios.get('/api/benh-nhan');
      setBenhNhans(res.data.data || []);
    } catch (error: any) {
      toast.error(`Lỗi: ${error.response?.data?.message || error.message}`);
    }
  }, [form, isEditing, benhNhans, generateNextMa]);

  const handleEdit = useCallback((bn: BenhNhan) => {
    setForm(bn);
    setIsEditing(true);
    setOpen(true);
  }, []);

  const handleDelete = useCallback(async (id: number) => {
    if (!window.confirm('Bạn có chắc chắn muốn xóa bệnh nhân này?')) return;
    try {
      await axios.delete(`/api/benh-nhan?id=${id}`);
      setBenhNhans((prev) => prev.filter((bn) => bn.id !== id));
      if (selectedBenhNhanId === id) {
        setSelectedBenhNhanId(null);
        setDonThuocs([]);
        setChiTietDonThuocs({});
        setDienTiens({});
      }
      toast.success('Đã xóa bệnh nhân');
    } catch (error: any) {
      toast.error(`Lỗi khi xóa bệnh nhân: ${error.response?.data?.message || error.message}`);
    }
  }, [selectedBenhNhanId]);

  const filtered = useMemo(
    () =>
      benhNhans.filter(
        (bn) =>
          bn.ten.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) ||
          bn.mabenhnhan.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase())
      ),
    [benhNhans, search]
  );

 // const totalPages = Math.ceil(filtered.length / rowsPerPage);
  const startIndex = (currentPage - 1) * rowsPerPage;
  const paginated = useMemo(
    () => filtered.slice(startIndex, startIndex + rowsPerPage),
    [filtered, startIndex, rowsPerPage]
  );

  // Danh sách chờ khám (tạm thời lấy 10 bệnh nhân đầu)
  const dsChoKham = useMemo(() => benhNhans.slice(0, 10), [benhNhans]);

  // Format lịch sử khám và đơn thuốc
  const filteredDonThuocs = useMemo(() => {
    return donThuocs.map((don) => {
      const chiTiet = chiTietDonThuocs[don.id] || [];
      const dieuTri = chiTiet
        .map((ct) => `${ct.thuoc.tenthuoc} x ${ct.soluong}`)
        .join(', ') || '-';
      const dienTien = (dienTiens[selectedBenhNhanId!] || []).find(
        (dt) => dt.ngay.slice(0, 10) === don.ngaylap.slice(0, 10)
      );
      return {
        ...don,
        dieuTri,
        dienTien: dienTien ? dienTien.noidung : '-',
      };
    });
  }, [donThuocs, chiTietDonThuocs, dienTiens, selectedBenhNhanId]);

  return (
    <div className="p-4">
      <Toaster position="top-right" />
      <div className="grid grid-cols-5 gap-4">
        {/* Danh sách chờ khám */}
        <div className="col-span-1">
          <Card>
            <CardContent className="p-2 space-y-2">
              <h2 className="font-semibold text-sm">Danh Sách Chờ Khám</h2>
              <div className="max-h-[70vh] overflow-y-auto">
                {dsChoKham.length === 0 && (
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Chưa có bệnh nhân chờ khám.</p>
                )}
                {dsChoKham.map((bn, idx) => (
                  <div
                    key={bn.id}
                    className="flex justify-between items-center border-b py-1 text-xs hover:bg-gray-100"
                  >
                    <div>
                      <p className="font-semibold">{idx + 1}. {bn.ten}</p>
                      <p className="text-muted-foreground">{bn.mabenhnhan}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex gap-1">
                      <Link href={`/ke-don?bn=${bn.id}`}>
                        <Button size="sm" className="text-xs px-2 py-1 bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700">
                          Kê Đơn
                        </Button>
                      </Link>
                      <Link href={`/ke-don-kinh?bn=${bn.id}`}>
                        <Button size="sm" className="text-xs px-2 py-1 bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700">
                          Kính
                        </Button>
                      </Link>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        </div>

        {/* Nội dung chính */}
        <div className="col-span-4 space-y-2">
          {/* Header */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold">Quản Lý Bệnh Nhân</h1>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <Input
                placeholder="Tìm kiếm bệnh nhân..."
                value={search}
                onChange={(e) => {
                  setSearch(e.target.value);
                  setCurrentPage(1);
                  setSelectedBenhNhanId(null);
                  setDonThuocs([]);
                  setChiTietDonThuocs({});
                  setDienTiens({});
                }}
                className="w-64 text-sm"
              />
              <Button
                size="sm"
                onClick={() => {
                  setIsEditing(false);
                  const nextMa = generateNextMa(benhNhans);
                  setForm({
                    mabenhnhan: nextMa,
                    ten: '',
                    namsinh: 2000,
                    gioitinh: 'Nam',
                    dienthoai: '',
                    diachi: '',
                  });
                  setOpen(true);
                }}
              >
                <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-1" /> Thêm
              </Button>
              <select
                value={rowsPerPage}
                onChange={(e) => {
                  setRowsPerPage(+e.target.value);
                  setCurrentPage(1);
                }}
                className="border px-2 py-1 rounded text-sm"
              >
                {[100, 200, 500, 1000].map((val) => (
                  <option key={val} value={val}>{val}</option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Tổng số bệnh nhân */}
          <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            Tổng cộng: {filtered.length} bệnh nhân
          </div>

          {/* Bảng bệnh nhân */}
          <Card>
            <CardContent className="p-0">
              <table className="min-w-full text-sm text-left">
                <thead className="bg-gray-100 border-b">
                  <tr>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1">Mã BN</th>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1">Họ Tên</th>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1">Năm Sinh</th>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1">Giới Tính</th>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1">Điện Thoại</th>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1">Địa Chỉ</th>
                    <th className="px-2 py-1 text-center">Hành Động</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                  {paginated.map((bn) => (
                    <React.Fragment key={bn.id}>
                      <tr className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
                        <td className="px-2 py-1 font-mono">{bn.mabenhnhan}</td>
                        <td
                          className="px-2 py-1 cursor-pointer text-black font-bold hover:text-blue-600"
                          onClick={() => handleSelectBenhNhan(bn.id!)}
                        >
                          {bn.ten}
                        </td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{bn.namsinh}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{bn.gioitinh}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{bn.dienthoai}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{bn.diachi}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1 text-center space-x-1">
                          <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => handleEdit(bn)}>
                            <Pencil className="w-3 h-3" />
                          </Button>
                          <Link href={`/ke-don?bn=${bn.id}`}>
                            <Button size="sm" className="bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700 text-white text-xs px-2 py-1">
                              Kê Đơn
                            </Button>
                          </Link>
                          <Link href={`/ke-don-kinh?bn=${bn.id}`}>
                            <Button size="sm" className="bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700 text-white text-xs px-2 py-1">
                              Kính
                            </Button>
                          </Link>
                          <Button size="sm" variant="destructive" onClick={() => handleDelete(bn.id!)}>
                            <Trash2 className="w-3 h-3" />
                          </Button>
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                      {selectedBenhNhanId === bn.id && (
                        <tr>
                          <td colSpan={7} className="px-2 py-1">
                            <Card className="shadow-sm bg-yellow-50">
                              <CardContent className="p-2">
                                {filteredDonThuocs.length === 0 ? (
                                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Chưa có đơn thuốc nào.</p>
                                ) : (
                                  <table className="min-w-full text-xs">
                                    <thead>
                                      <tr className="border-b">
                                        <th className="text-left py-1">Ngày khám</th>
                                        <th className="text-left py-1">Chẩn đoán</th>
                                        <th className="text-left py-1 max-w-[200px]">Điều trị (thuốc, số lượng)</th>
                                        <th className="text-left py-1 max-w-[200px]">Diễn tiến bệnh</th>
                                        <th className="text-right py-1">Số tiền</th>
                                      </tr>
                                    </thead>
                                    <tbody>
                                      {filteredDonThuocs.map((don) => (
                                        <tr key={don.id} className="border-b">
                                          <td className="py-1">
                                            {new Date(don.ngaylap).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')}
                                          </td>
                                          <td className="py-1">{don.chandoan}</td>
                                          <td className="py-1 truncate">{don.dieuTri}</td>
                                          <td className="py-1 truncate">{don.dienTien}</td>
                                          <td className="text-right py-1">
                                            {(don.tongtien / 1000).toFixed(0)}k
                                          </td>
                                        </tr>
                                      ))}
                                    </tbody>
                                  </table>
                                )}
                              </CardContent>
                            </Card>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      )}
                    </React.Fragment>
                  ))}
                  {paginated.length === 0 && (
                    <tr>
                      <td colSpan={7} className="text-center py-2 text-muted-foreground">
                        Không tìm thấy bệnh nhân.
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  )}
                </tbody>
              </table>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>

          {/* Phân trang */}
          <div className="flex justify-center gap-1 mt-2">
            {[...Array(totalPages)].map((_, i) => (
              <button
                key={i + 1}
                onClick={() => {
                  setCurrentPage(i + 1);
                  setSelectedBenhNhanId(null);
                  setDonThuocs([]);
                  setChiTietDonThuocs({});
                  setDienTiens({});
                }}
                className={`px-2 py-1 border rounded text-sm ${
                  currentPage === i + 1 ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'hover:bg-blue-100'
                }`}
              >
                {i + 1}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Popup Dialog */}
      <Dialog open={open} onOpenChange={setOpen}>
        <DialogContent>
          <DialogHeader>
            <DialogTitle>{isEditing ? 'Sửa Bệnh Nhân' : 'Thêm Bệnh Nhân'}</DialogTitle>
          </DialogHeader>
          <div className="space-y-2 py-2">
            <Label>Mã Bệnh Nhân</Label>
            <Input value={form.mabenhnhan} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, mabenhnhan: e.target.value })} />
            <Label>Họ Tên *</Label>
            <Input value={form.ten} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, ten: e.target.value })} />
            <Label>Năm Sinh *</Label>
            <Input type="number" value={form.namsinh} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, namsinh: +e.target.value })} />
            <Label>Giới Tính</Label>
            <select
              className="w-full border rounded p-2 text-sm"
              value={form.gioitinh}
              onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, gioitinh: e.target.value })}
            >
              <option value="Nam">Nam</option>
              <option value="Nữ">Nữ</option>
            </select>
            <Label>Điện Thoại</Label>
            <Input value={form.dienthoai} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, dienthoai: e.target.value })} />
            <Label>Địa Chỉ *</Label>
            <Input value={form.diachi} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, diachi: e.target.value })} />
          </div>
          <DialogFooter className="mt-2">
            <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setOpen(false)}>
              Hủy
            </Button>
            <Button onClick={handleSubmit}>Lưu</Button>
          </DialogFooter>
        </DialogContent>
      </Dialog>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## File: src\pages\don-kinh.tsx

```tsx
'use client';

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Card, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Trash2, Pencil } from 'lucide-react';
import { Switch } from '@/components/ui/switch';
import toast, { Toaster } from 'react-hot-toast';

interface DonKinh {
  id: number;
  benhnhanid: number;
  chandoan: string;
  ngaykham: string;
  giatrong: number;
  giagong: number;
  ghichu: string | null;
  thiluc_khongkinh_mp: string | null;
  thiluc_kinhcu_mp: string | null;
  thiluc_kinhmoi_mp: string | null;
  sokinh_cu_mp: string | null;
  sokinh_moi_mp: string | null;
  hangtrong_mp: string | null;
  ax_mp: number | null;
  thiluc_khongkinh_mt: string | null;
  thiluc_kinhcu_mt: string | null;
  thiluc_kinhmoi_mt: string | null;
  sokinh_cu_mt: string | null;
  sokinh_moi_mt: string | null;
  hangtrong_mt: string | null;
  ax_mt: number | null;
  no: boolean;
  sotienno: number;
  lai: number;
  benhnhan: {
    id: number;
    ten: string | null;
    namsinh: number;
    dienthoai: string | null;
    diachi: string | null;
  };
}

interface BenhNhan {
  id: number;
  mabenhnhan: string | null;
  ten: string | null;
  namsinh: number;
  gioitinh: string | null;
  dienthoai: string | null;
  diachi: string | null;
}

export default function DonKinhPage() {
  const [donKinhs, setDonKinhs] = useState<DonKinh[]>([]);
  const [benhNhans, setBenhNhans] = useState<BenhNhan[]>([]);
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const [dateFilter, setDateFilter] = useState('');
  const [debtFilter, setDebtFilter] = useState<boolean | null>(null);
  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1);
  const [rowsPerPage] = useState(10);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchData = async () => {
      setIsLoading(true);
      try {
        const resDonKinh = await axios.get('/api/don-kinh');
        setDonKinhs(resDonKinh.data.data || []);
        const resBenhNhan = await axios.get('/api/benh-nhan');
        setBenhNhans(resBenhNhan.data.data || []);
      } catch (error: any) {
        const errorMessage = error.response?.data?.message || 'Lỗi không xác định';
        const errorDetails = error.response?.data?.details || '';
        toast.error(`Lỗi khi tải dữ liệu: ${errorMessage}${errorDetails ? ' - ' + errorDetails : ''}`);
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    };
    fetchData();
  }, []);

  const handleDelete = async (id: number) => {
    if (!confirm('Bạn có chắc muốn xóa đơn kính này?')) return;
    try {
      const res = await axios.delete(`/api/don-kinh?id=${id}`);
      if (res.status === 200) {
        setDonKinhs(donKinhs.filter((dk) => dk.id !== id));
        toast.success('Đã xóa đơn kính');
      }
    } catch (error: any) {
      const errorMessage = error.response?.data?.message || 'Lỗi không xác định';
      const errorDetails = error.response?.data?.details || '';
      toast.error(`Lỗi khi xóa đơn kính: ${errorMessage}${errorDetails ? ' - ' + errorDetails : ''}`);
    }
  };

  const filtered = donKinhs.filter((dk) => {
    const searchLower = search.toLowerCase();
    const matchSearch =
      (dk.benhnhan.ten && dk.benhnhan.ten.toLowerCase().includes(searchLower)) ||
      (dk.benhnhan.dienthoai && dk.benhnhan.dienthoai.includes(searchLower)) ||
      (dk.benhnhan.diachi && dk.benhnhan.diachi.toLowerCase().includes(searchLower));
    const matchDate = dateFilter ? dk.ngaykham.startsWith(dateFilter) : true;
    const matchDebt = debtFilter !== null ? dk.sotienno > 0 : true;
    return (matchSearch || !search || searchLower === '') && matchDate && matchDebt;
  });

  const totalPages = Math.ceil(filtered.length / rowsPerPage);
  const startIndex = (currentPage - 1) * rowsPerPage;
  const paginated = filtered.slice(startIndex, startIndex + rowsPerPage);

  const formatMoney = (amount: number) => {
    return (amount / 1000).toLocaleString('vi-VN');
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-6 space-y-4">
      <Toaster position="top-right" />
      {isLoading ? (
        <div className="text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">Đang tải dữ liệu...</div>
      ) : (
        <>
          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-4 items-center">
            <Input
              placeholder="Tìm tên, số ĐT, địa chỉ..."
              value={search}
              onChange={(e) => {
                setSearch(e.target.value);
                setCurrentPage(1);
              }}
              className="w-full sm:w-1/3"
            />
            <Input
              type="date"
              value={dateFilter}
              onChange={(e) => {
                setDateFilter(e.target.value);
                setCurrentPage(1);
              }}
              className="w-full sm:w-1/4"
            />
            <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
              <Switch
                checked={debtFilter === true}
                onCheckedChange={(checked) => {
                  setDebtFilter(checked ? true : null);
                  setCurrentPage(1);
                }}
              />
              <label className="text-sm font-semibold">Chỉ hiển thị đơn còn nợ</label>
            </div>
            <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground whitespace-nowrap">
              Tổng cộng: {filtered.length} đơn kính
            </div>
          </div>

          <Card>
            <CardContent className="p-0 overflow-x-auto">
              <table className="min-w-full text-sm text-left">
                <thead className="bg-gray-100 border-b">
                  <tr>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2">Ngày khám</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2">Họ tên</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2">NS</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2">Điện thoại</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2">Địa chỉ</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2">Mắt phải</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2">Mắt trái</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2">Tổng tiền</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2">Nợ</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-center">Hành động</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                  {paginated.map((dk) => (
                    <tr key={dk.id} className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
                      <td className="px-4 py-2">{new Date(dk.ngaykham).toLocaleDateString()}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2">{dk.benhnhan.ten || '-'}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2">{dk.benhnhan.namsinh}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2">{dk.benhnhan.dienthoai || '-'}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2">{dk.benhnhan.diachi || '-'}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2">{dk.sokinh_moi_mp || '-'}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2">{dk.sokinh_moi_mt || '-'}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2">{formatMoney(dk.giatrong + dk.giagong)}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2">{dk.sotienno > 0 ? formatMoney(dk.sotienno) : '-'}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2 text-center space-x-2">
                        <Button size="sm" variant="outline" asChild>
                          <a href={`/ke-don-kinh?bn=${dk.benhnhanid}`}>
                            <Pencil className="w-4 h-4" />
                          </a>
                        </Button>
                        <Button size="sm" variant="destructive" onClick={() => handleDelete(dk.id)}>
                          <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />
                        </Button>
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  ))}
                  {paginated.length === 0 && (
                    <tr>
                      <td colSpan={10} className="text-center py-4 text-muted-foreground">
                        Không tìm thấy đơn kính.
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  )}
                </tbody>
              </table>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>

          <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-4">
            {[...Array(totalPages)].map((_, i) => (
              <button
                key={i + 1}
                onClick={() => setCurrentPage(i + 1)}
                className={`px-3 py-1 border rounded ${currentPage === i + 1 ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'hover:bg-blue-100'}`}
              >
                {i + 1}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

## File: src\pages\don-thuoc.tsx

```tsx
'use client';

import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback, useMemo } from 'react';
import { Input } from '../components/ui/input';
import { Button } from '../components/ui/button';
import { Card, CardContent } from '../components/ui/card';
import { Pencil, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';
import axios from 'axios';
import toast, { Toaster } from 'react-hot-toast';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { format } from 'date-fns';

interface DonThuoc {
  id: number;
  madonthuoc: string;
  benhnhan: {
    id: number;
    mabenhnhan: string;
    ten: string | null;
    namsinh: number | null;
    dienthoai: string | null;
    diachi: string | null;
  };
  chandoan: string;
  chuyen_khoa: string | null;
  ngaylap: string;
  tongtien: number;
  sotien_da_thanh_toan: number;
  trangthai_thanh_toan: string;
}

interface ChiTietDonThuoc {
  thuoc: {
    id: number;
    tenthuoc: string;
  };
  soluong: number;
  donvitinh: string;
  cachdung: string;
}

export default function DonThuocPage() {
  const [donThuocs, setDonThuocs] = useState<DonThuoc[]>([]);
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const [filterDate, setFilterDate] = useState('');
  const [filterNo, setFilterNo] = useState(false);
  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1);
  const [rowsPerPage, setRowsPerPage] = useState(10);
  const [chiTietDonThuocs, setChiTietDonThuocs] = useState<{ [donthuocid: number]: ChiTietDonThuoc[] }>({});
  const [selectedDonThuocId, setSelectedDonThuocId] = useState<number | null>(null);

  // Fetch danh sách đơn thuốc
  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchDonThuocs = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await axios.get('/api/don-thuoc');
        const data = res.data.data || [];
        // Kiểm tra và lọc dữ liệu không hợp lệ
        const validData = data.filter((dt: DonThuoc) => 
          dt && dt.benhnhan && (dt.benhnhan.ten === null || typeof dt.benhnhan.ten === 'string')
        );
        setDonThuocs(validData);
        if (data.length !== validData.length) {
          toast.error('Một số đơn thuốc có dữ liệu không hợp lệ đã bị lọc bỏ');
        }
      } catch (error: any) {
        toast.error(`Lỗi tải danh sách đơn thuốc: ${error.response?.data?.message || error.message}`);
      }
    };
    fetchDonThuocs();
  }, []);

  // Fetch chi tiết đơn thuốc
  const fetchChiTietDonThuoc = useCallback(async (donthuocid: number) => {
    try {
      const res = await axios.get(`/api/chi-tiet-don-thuoc?donthuocid=${donthuocid}`);
      setChiTietDonThuocs((prev) => ({
        ...prev,
        [donthuocid]: res.data.data.map((item: any) => ({
          thuoc: { id: item.thuoc.id, tenthuoc: item.thuoc.tenthuoc },
          soluong: item.soluong,
          donvitinh: item.donvitinh || 'N/A',
          cachdung: item.cachdung || 'N/A',
        })),
      }));
    } catch (error: any) {
      toast.error(`Lỗi tải chi tiết đơn thuốc: ${error.response?.data?.message || error.message}`);
    }
  }, []);

  const handleDelete = useCallback(async (id: number) => {
    if (!window.confirm('Bạn có chắc chắn muốn xóa đơn thuốc này?')) return;
    try {
      await axios.delete(`/api/don-thuoc?id=${id}`);
      setDonThuocs((prev) => prev.filter((dt) => dt.id !== id));
      setChiTietDonThuocs((prev) => {
        const newState = { ...prev };
        delete newState[id];
        return newState;
      });
      if (selectedDonThuocId === id) setSelectedDonThuocId(null);
      toast.success('Đã xóa đơn thuốc');
    } catch (error: any) {
      toast.error(`Lỗi xóa đơn thuốc: ${error.response?.data?.message || error.message}`);
    }
  }, [selectedDonThuocId]);

  const handleRowClick = useCallback((donthuocid: number) => {
    if (selectedDonThuocId === donthuocid) {
      setSelectedDonThuocId(null); // Ẩn chi tiết nếu bấm lại
    } else {
      setSelectedDonThuocId(donthuocid);
      fetchChiTietDonThuoc(donthuocid);
    }
  }, [selectedDonThuocId, fetchChiTietDonThuoc]);

  const filteredDonThuocs = useMemo(() => {
    return donThuocs
      .filter((dt) => {
        const searchLower = search.toLowerCase();
        const matchesSearch =
          (dt.benhnhan?.ten && dt.benhnhan.ten.toLowerCase().includes(searchLower)) ||
          (dt.benhnhan?.mabenhnhan && dt.benhnhan.mabenhnhan.toLowerCase().includes(searchLower)) ||
          (dt.benhnhan?.dienthoai && dt.benhnhan.dienthoai.includes(searchLower)) ||
          (dt.benhnhan?.diachi && dt.benhnhan.diachi.toLowerCase().includes(searchLower));
        const matchesDate = filterDate ? dt.ngaylap?.startsWith(filterDate) : true;
        const matchesNo = filterNo ? dt.trangthai_thanh_toan === 'nợ' : true;
        return matchesSearch && matchesDate && matchesNo;
      })
      .sort((a, b) => new Date(b.ngaylap).getTime() - new Date(a.ngaylap).getTime());
  }, [donThuocs, search, filterDate, filterNo]);

  const totalPages = Math.ceil(filteredDonThuocs.length / rowsPerPage);
  const startIndex = (currentPage - 1) * rowsPerPage;
  const paginatedDonThuocs = useMemo(
    () => filteredDonThuocs.slice(startIndex, startIndex + rowsPerPage),
    [filteredDonThuocs, startIndex, rowsPerPage]
  );

  return (
    <div className="p-4">
      <Toaster position="top-right" />
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Input
              placeholder="Tìm theo tên, mã BN, SĐT, địa chỉ..."
              value={search}
              onChange={(e) => {
                setSearch(e.target.value);
                setCurrentPage(1);
              }}
              className="w-64"
            />
            <Input
              type="date"
              value={filterDate}
              onChange={(e) => {
                setFilterDate(e.target.value);
                setCurrentPage(1);
              }}
              className="w-40"
            />
            <Button
              variant={filterNo ? 'default' : 'outline'}
              onClick={() => {
                setFilterNo(!filterNo);
                setCurrentPage(1);
              }}
            >
              Chỉ hiện đơn còn nợ
            </Button>
          </div>
          <select
            value={rowsPerPage}
            onChange={(e) => {
              setRowsPerPage(+e.target.value);
              setCurrentPage(1);
            }}
            className="border px-2 py-1 rounded text-sm"
          >
            {[10, 20, 50, 100].map((val) => (
              <option key={val} value={val}>{val}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        <Card>
          <CardContent className="p-0">
            <table className="min-w-full text-sm">
              <thead className="bg-gray-100">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Ngày</th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Bệnh Nhân</th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">NS</th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">SĐT</th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Địa chỉ</th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Chẩn Đoán</th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Khoa</th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-right">Tổng Tiền</th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-right">Nợ</th>
                  <th className="px-2 py-1 text-center">Hành Động</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                {paginatedDonThuocs.map((dt) => {
                  const chiTiet = chiTietDonThuocs[dt.id] || [];
                  return (
                    <React.Fragment key={dt.id}>
                      <tr
                        className="border-b hover:bg-gray-100 cursor-pointer"
                        onClick={() => handleRowClick(dt.id)}
                      >
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{format(new Date(dt.ngaylap), 'dd/MM/yyyy')}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{dt.benhnhan?.ten || '-'}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{dt.benhnhan?.namsinh || '-'}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{dt.benhnhan?.dienthoai || '-'}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{dt.benhnhan?.diachi || '-'}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{dt.chandoan || '-'}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1">{dt.chuyen_khoa || '-'}</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{(dt.tongtien / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1 text-right">{((dt.tongtien - dt.sotien_da_thanh_toan) / 1000).toFixed(0)}k</td>
                        <td className="px-2 py-1 text-center space-x-1">
                          <Link href={`/ke-don?bn=${dt.benhnhan?.id || ''}&donthuocid=${dt.id}`}>
                            <Button size="sm" variant="outline">
                              <Pencil className="w-3 h-3" />
                            </Button>
                          </Link>
                          <Button
                            size="sm"
                            variant="destructive"
                            onClick={(e) => {
                              e.stopPropagation();
                              handleDelete(dt.id);
                            }}
                          >
                            <Trash2 className="w-3 h-3" />
                          </Button>
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                      {chiTiet.length > 0 && selectedDonThuocId === dt.id && (
                        <tr>
                          <td colSpan={10} className="px-2 py-1 bg-green-50">
                            <div className="text-xs text-gray-800">
                              <strong>Chi tiết đơn thuốc:</strong>
                              <table className="min-w-full text-xs mt-2">
                                <thead>
                                  <tr className="bg-green-100">
                                    <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Tên Thuốc</th>
                                    <th className="px-2 py-1 text-center">Số Lượng</th>
                                    <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Đơn Vị</th>
                                    <th className="px-2 py-1 text-left">Cách Dùng</th>
                                  </tr>
                                </thead>
                                <tbody>
                                  {chiTiet.map((ct) => (
                                    <tr key={ct.thuoc.id} className="border-b">
                                      <td className="px-2 py-1">{ct.thuoc.tenthuoc}</td>
                                      <td className="px-2 py-1 text-center">{ct.soluong}</td>
                                      <td className="px-2 py-1">{ct.donvitinh}</td>
                                      <td className="px-2 py-1">{ct.cachdung}</td>
                                    </tr>
                                  ))}
                                </tbody>
                              </table>
                            </div>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      )}
                    </React.Fragment>
                  );
                })}
                {paginatedDonThuocs.length === 0 && (
                  <tr>
                    <td colSpan={10} className="text-center py-2 text-muted-foreground">
                      Không tìm thấy đơn thuốc.
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                )}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        <div className="flex justify-center gap-1 mt-4">
          {[...Array(totalPages)].map((_, i) => (
            <button
              key={i + 1}
              onClick={() => setCurrentPage(i + 1)}
              className={`px-2 py-1 border rounded text-sm ${
                currentPage === i + 1 ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'hover:bg-gray-100'
              }`}
            >
              {i + 1}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```
